cp-subnav-group-link-icon"><svg data-icon="dot" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><desc>dot</desc><path d="M8 5a3 3 0 100 6 3 3 0 100-6z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></span>Bar Chart</a></li></ul></li></ol></nav><div class="cp-subnav-dummy is-hidden" style="height: 45px;"></div><div class="cp-section Section about "><h2 class="section-title"><a class="anchor" href="#about" id="about">About</a></h2><div class="section-body"><div class="section-content"><div class="section-description"><div><p>Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations are most often employed by the&nbsp;<a href="/profile/naics/6111">Elementary &amp; secondary schools</a>&nbsp;industry. The average yearly wage for Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations was&nbsp;$81,575 in&nbsp;2016. The top 3 most similar occupations to Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations by wage are&nbsp;<a href="/profile/soc/550000">Military specific occupations</a>, <a href="/profile/soc/450000-490000">Natural resources, construction, &amp; maintenance occupations</a>, and <a href="/profile/soc/410000-430000">Sales &amp; Office Occupations</a>.</p></div><div><p>The top 3 locations that employ the most Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations are <a href="/profile/geo/79500US1100105">District of Columbia (Central) PUMA, DC</a>, <a href="/profile/geo/79500US3603805">Upper East Side PUMA, NY</a>, and <a href="/profile/geo/79500US1703502">Lake View &amp; Lincoln Park PUMA, IL</a>. The top 3 locations with a&nbsp;relatively high concentration of Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations are <a href="/profile/geo/79500US1100101">District of Columbia (West) PUMA, DC</a>, <a href="/profile/geo/79500US1100105">District of Columbia (Central) PUMA, DC</a>, and <a href="/profile/geo/79500US0608501">Mountain View, Palo Alto &amp; Los Altos Cities PUMA, CA</a>.</p></div></div><div class="section-visualizations"><a class="photo-attribution" href="https://flic.kr/p/hT9nnA" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span icon="camera" class="bp3-icon bp3-icon-camera"><svg data-icon="camera" width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><desc>camera</desc><path d="M15 3h-2.59L10.7 1.29A.956.956 0 0010 1H6c-.28 0-.53.11-.71.29L3.59 3H1c-.55 0-1 .45-1 1v7c0 .55.45 1 1 1h2.56c1.1 1.22 2.67 2 4.44 2s3.34-.78 4.44-2H15c.55 0 1-.45 1-1V4c0-.55-.45-1-1-1zM3 6H1V5h2v1zm5 6c-2.21 0-4-1.79-4-4s1.79-4 4-4 4 1.79 4 4-1.79 4-4 4zm0-6c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2s.9 2 2 2 2-.9 2-2-.9-2-2-2z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></span>Photo by <!-- -->reynermedia</a></div></div></div><div class="section-topics"></div></div><div class="cp-section Section employment "><h2 class="section-title"><span icon="briefcase" class="bp3-icon bp3-icon-briefcase"><svg data-icon="briefcase" width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><desc>briefcase</desc><path d="M19 5h-4V2c0-.55-.45-1-1-1H6c-.55 0-1 .45-1 1v3H1c-.55 0-1 .45-1 1v5h4v-1h2v1h8v-1h2v1h4V6c0-.55-.45-1-1-1zm-6 0H7V3h6v2zm3 8h-2v-1H6v1H4v-1H0v6c0 .55.45 1 1 1h18c.55 0 1-.45 1-1v-6h-4v1z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></span><a class="anchor" href="#employment" id="employment">Employment</a></h2><div class="section-body"><div class="section-content"><div class="section-description"><div><p>Information on the businesses and industries that employ Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations and on wages and locations for those in the field.&nbsp;<a href="/profile/naics/6111">Elementary &amp; secondary schools</a> is the industry that employs the most Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations, both by share and by number, though the highest paid industry for Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations, by average wage, is <a href="/profile/naics/51913">Internet publishing, broadcasting &amp; web search portals</a>. Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations are paid most in <a href="/profile/geo/79500US3603810">Battery Park City, Greenwich Village &amp; Soho PUMA, NY</a> but are relatively concentrated in <a href="/profile/geo/79500US1100101">District of Columbia (West) PUMA, DC</a>.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="section-topics"><div class="topic wage_by_industry TextViz "><div class="topic-content"><h4 id="wage_by_industry" class="topic-title"><a class="anchor" href="#wage_by_industry">Yearly Wage</a></h4><div class="topic-stats"><div class="StatGroup single"><div class="stat-value">$81,575</div><div class="stat-title">AVERAGE SALARY</div><div class="stat-subtitle"><span class="plus-minus">±</span> $268</div></div></div><div class="topic-descriptions"><div class="topic-description"><p>In&nbsp;2020, Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations earned an average of&nbsp;$81,575, $25,621 more than than the average national salary of $55,954.</p></div><div class="topic-description"><p>Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations are the highest paid occupation in the US followed by&nbsp;<a href="/profile/soc/550000">Military specific occupations</a>. This chart shows the various occupations closest to Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations as measured by average annual salary in the US.</p></div></div></div><div class="visualization topic-visualization"><div class="Options"><span class="bp3-popover-wrapper"><span class="bp3-popover-target"><div class="option view-table" tabindex="0"><span class="option-label">View Data</span></div></span></span><span class="bp3-popover-wrapper"><span class="bp3-popover-target"><div class="option save-image" tabindex="0"><span class="option-label">Save Image</span></div></span></span><span class="bp3-popover-wrapper"><span class="bp3-popover-target"><div class="option share" tabindex="0"><span class="option-label">Share / Embed</span></div></span></span><span class="bp3-popover-wrapper"><span class="bp3-popover-target"><div class="option add-to-cart " tabindex="0"><span class="option-label">Add Data to Cart</span></div></span></span></div><div class="d3plus" style="position: relative;"><svg class="d3plus-viz" aria-hidden="true" aria-labelledby="0f9ea2c3-db25-f305-cfbe-34f40ab882ef-title 0f9ea2c3-db25-f305-cfbe-34f40ab882ef-desc" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" opacity="1"><title id="0f9ea2c3-db25-f305-cfbe-34f40ab882ef-title"></title><desc id="0f9ea2c3-db25-f305-cfbe-34f40ab882ef-desc"></desc></svg></div></div></div><div class="topic wage_distribution TextViz "><div class="topic-content"><h4 id="wage_distribution" class="topic-title"><a class="anchor" href="#wage_distribution">Wage Distribution</a></h4><div class="topic-stats"><div class="StatGroup single"><div class="stat-value">0.43</div><div class="stat-title">WAGE&nbsp;GINI</div><div class="stat-subtitle"></div></div></div><div class="topic-descriptions"><div class="topic-description"><p>In 2015, Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations had a wage&nbsp;GINI&nbsp;coefficient of 0.43, which is lower than than the national average of 0.478. In other words, wages are distributed more evenly for Management, business, science, &amp; arts occupations (shown in red) than for the overall labor force (shown in gray).</p></div></div></div><div
